# ::id tatoeba_nor.1 ::eng He does n't have the ability to do the work properly .
# ::snt Han er ikke i stand til å gjøre arbeidet skikkelig .
# ::snt He does n't have the ability to do the work properly .
(c / capable-01
      :polarity -
      :ARG1 (h / he)
      :ARG2 (w / work-01
            :ARG0 h
            :manner (p / proper)))

# ::id tatoeba_nor.2 ::eng Do you know what this box is made of ?

      :ARG1 (t / thing
            :ARG2-of (m / make-01
                  :ARG1 (b / box
                        :mod (t2 / this))))
      :polarity (a / amr-unknown))

                        :value 1)))
      :ARG1 h
      :time (d / date-entity
            :dayperiod (m / morning)
            :mod (t / today)))
